# Azure Icons Inventory

> **Source:** [maskati/azure-icons](https://github.com/maskati/azure-icons) (mirrors [iconcloud.design](https://iconcloud.design/browse/Azure%20Icons))
> **Total:** 1427 icons across 350 extensions
> **CDN Base URL:** `https://raw.githubusercontent.com/maskati/azure-icons/main/svg/{Extension}/{IconName}.svg`
